	desc = "HIDDEN TECHS"

			limit = {
				OR = {

					}
					AND = {

						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 5 }

					AND = {

					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 0
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 1 }
					}				
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 1
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 2 }
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 2
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 3 }
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 3
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 4 }
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 4
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 5 }
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 5
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 6 }
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 6
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 7 }
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 7
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 8 }
					}
					AND = {
						game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 8
						NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 9 }
					}
				}
			}
			game_balance_tech_stage_4 = 4500
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "game_balance_tech_stage_4_cooldown"
				duration = 118
			}
			#GER = { country_event = 650020 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "game_balance_tech_stage_4_cooldown"
			duration = 118
		}
	}
}

province_event = { 				
	id = 530010
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	trigger = {	
		not = { check_variable = { which = "GBP_experience" value = 150 } }
		war = yes
		not = { grand_battle_plan = 1 }
        not = { has_country_modifier = GBP_experience_CD }
		any_neighbor_province = { 
			controller = {
				grand_battle_plan = 1 
				war_with = THIS
			}
		}
		last_battle_loser_losses = 1000
		not = { last_battle_loser_losses = 2000 }
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME530013"
	desc = "EVTDESC530013"
	picture = "doctrine_learn"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA530013"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		THIS = {
			any_controlled = { 
				limit = { 
					country_units_in_province = THIS 
					units_in_province = 1
					any_neighbor_province  = {
						limit = { 
							controller = { 
								grand_battle_plan = 1 
								war_with = THIS
								not = { 
									blitzkrieg = 1
									superior_firepower = 1
									deep_battle_doctrine = 1
								}
							} 
							units_in_province = 1 
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = learn_grand_battle_plan_province_flag_2
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { 
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_I"
						duration = 1		
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_CD"
						duration = 7		
					}
					change_variable = { which = "GBP_experience" value = +5 }
				}
				25 = { 
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_II"
						duration = 1		
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_CD"
						duration = 7		
					}
					change_variable = { which = "GBP_experience" value = +7 }
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = 530006
		GER = { country_event = 530006 } # TEST

	}	
}

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		THIS = {

				limit = {

					units_in_province = 1

							controller = { 
								superior_firepower = 1 
								war_with = THIS
								not = {
									blitzkrieg = 1
									deep_battle_doctrine = 1
									grand_battle_plan = 1

							}

### VICTORY EVENTS

province_event = { 				
	id = 530050
	
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	trigger = {	
		not = { check_variable = { which = "GBP_experience" value = 150 } }
		war = yes
		not = { grand_battle_plan = 1 }
        not = { has_country_modifier = GBP_experience_CD }
		any_neighbor_province = { 
			controller = {
				grand_battle_plan = 1 
				war_with = THIS
			}
		}
		last_battle_winner_losses = 2000
		not = { last_battle_winner_losses = 3000 }
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME530033"
	desc = "EVTDESC530033"
	picture = "doctrine_learn"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA530013"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		THIS = {
			any_controlled = { 
				limit = { 
					country_units_in_province = THIS 
					units_in_province = 1
					any_neighbor_province  = {
						limit = { 
							controller = { 
								grand_battle_plan = 1 
								war_with = THIS
								not = { 
									blitzkrieg = 1
									superior_firepower = 1
									deep_battle_doctrine = 1
								}
							} 
							units_in_province = 1 
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { 
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_I"
						duration = 1		
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_CD"
						duration = 7		
					}
					change_variable = { which = "GBP_experience" value = +5 }
				}
				25 = { 
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_II"
						duration = 1		
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = "GBP_experience_CD"
						duration = 7		
					}
					change_variable = { which = "GBP_experience" value = +7 }
				}
			}
		}		
		country_event = 530006
		GER = { country_event = 530006 } # TEST
	}	
}

######################################################
############   Resource Trade Cooldowns   ############
######################################################	

country_event = { # LVL 1
	id = 969700
	
	trigger = {
		ENG = { 
			check_variable = { which = "trade_resource_chromite_ENG" value = 0.01 } 
			not = { check_variable = { which = "trade_resource_chromite_ENG" value = 1.01 } }
		}
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_I }
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_II }
		has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	title = "Trade Deal Closed"
	desc = "Trade deal will last for one year. Over this period of time United Kingdom will supply us with constant stream of Chromite."
	picture = "chromium_trade"

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_I"
			duration = 460
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

			check_variable = { which = "trade_resource_copper_CAN" value = 0.01 } 
			not = { check_variable = { which = "trade_resource_copper_CAN" value = 1.01 } }
		}
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_copper_CAN_cooldown_I }
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_copper_CAN_cooldown_II }
		has_country_modifier = buy_resource_copper_CAN
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	title = "Trade Deal Closed"
	desc = "Trade deal will last for one year. Over this period of time Canada will supply us with constant stream of Copper."
	picture = "copper_trade"

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "buy_resource_copper_CAN_cooldown_I"
			duration = 460
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = 969760
	
	trigger = {
		not = { has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG }
		or = {
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_I
			has_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_II
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	title = "Trade Expired"
	desc = "Our trade deal for Chromite with United Kingdom has expired. We need to refresh it or find different source."
	picture = "chromium_trade_expired"

	option = {
		name = "Time to browse our options again."
		ENG = { change_variable = { which = "trade_resource_chromite_ENG" value = -1 } }	
		remove_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_I
		remove_country_modifier = buy_resource_chromite_ENG_cooldown_II		
	}
}

	id = 7900
	
	trigger = {
		ai = no
		not = { has_country_flag = pay_goddamn_rent_start }
		or = {
			has_country_flag = BlackICE
			has_country_flag = Multiplayer
		}
	}
	
	title = "Budget limitations heads up"
	desc = "EVTDESC7900"
	picture = "salary_events"
	
	option = {
		name = "Time to prepare our budget."
		set_country_flag = pay_goddamn_rent_start
	}
}

country_event = { #1st
	id = 7901
	
	trigger = {
		ai = no
		has_country_flag = pay_goddamn_rent_start
		or = {
			has_country_flag = BlackICE
			has_country_flag = Multiplayer
		}
		or = {
			and = {
				or = {
					faction = axis
					tag = CHI
				}
				total_amount_of_brigades = 1000				
				not = { total_amount_of_brigades = 1100 }
			}
			and = {
				faction = comintern
				total_amount_of_brigades = 1700
				not = { total_amount_of_brigades = 1800 }
			}
			and = {
				or = {
					faction = allies
					and = {
						not = { faction = allies }
						not = { faction = axis }
						not = { faction = comintern }
						not = { tag = CHI }
					}
				}	
				total_amount_of_brigades = 700
				not = { total_amount_of_brigades = 800 }
			}
		}
		not = { 
			has_country_modifier = pay_soldiers_cooldown
		}
	}
	
	title = "Our Army asks for more money"
	desc = "EVTDESC7901"
	picture = "salary_events"
	
	option = {
		name = "OK - pay this time"
		money = -450
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "pay_soldiers_I"
			duration = 90
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "pay_soldiers_cooldown"
			duration = 90
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "NO - don't pay this time"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "pay_soldiers_I_NO"
			duration = 90
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "pay_soldiers_cooldown"
			duration = 90
		}
	}
}

	}

country_event = {
	id = 41306

	title = "TRAINING LAW start"
	desc = "Minimal to basic"
	picture = "doctrine_learn"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "ELITE"
			
			
			OMG = {
			
				### LAND ###
				
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						or = {
							and = {
								minimal_training_land_tech = 1
								not = { has_country_flag = units_training_law_START }
								not = { training_laws = minimal_training }
								training_laws = basic_training
							}
							and = {
								has_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag
								not = { training_laws = minimal_training }
								training_laws = basic_training
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = units_training_law_START 
					set_country_flag = basic_training_land_tech_flag
					clr_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag		
					minimal_training_land_tech_revert = 25000
					basic_training_land_tech = 25000
				}
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						or = {
							and = {
								minimal_training_land_tech = 1
								not = { has_country_flag = units_training_law_START }
								not = { training_laws = minimal_training }
								training_laws = advanced_training
							}
							and = {
								has_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag
								not = { training_laws = minimal_training }
								training_laws = advanced_training
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = units_training_law_START 
					set_country_flag = advanced_training_land_tech_flag
					clr_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag		
					minimal_training_land_tech_revert = 25000
					advanced_training_land_tech = 25000
				}
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						or = {
							and = {
								minimal_training_land_tech = 1
								not = { has_country_flag = units_training_law_START }
								not = { training_laws = minimal_training }
								training_laws = specialist_training
							}
							and = {
								has_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag 
								not = { training_laws = minimal_training }
								training_laws = specialist_training
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = units_training_law_START 
					set_country_flag = specialist_training_land_tech_flag
					clr_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag			
					minimal_training_land_tech_revert = 25000
					specialist_training_land_tech = 25000
				}
				
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						or = {
							and = {
								basic_training_land_tech = 1
								not = { has_country_flag = units_training_law_START }
								not = { training_laws = basic_training }
								training_laws = minimal_training
							}
							and = {
								has_country_flag = basic_training_land_tech_flag 
								not = { training_laws = basic_training }
								training_laws = minimal_training
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = units_training_law_START 
					set_country_flag = minimal_training_land_tech_flag
					clr_country_flag = basic_training_land_tech_flag
					basic_training_land_tech_revert = 25000
					minimal_training_land_tech = 25000
				}
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						or = {
							and ={
								basic_training_land_tech = 1
								not = { has_country_flag = units_training_law_START }
								not = { training_laws = basic_training }
								training_laws = advanced_training
							}
							and ={
								has_country_flag = basic_training_land_tech_flag
								not = { training_laws = basic_training }
								training_laws = advanced_training
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = units_training_law_START 
					set_country_flag = advanced_training_land_tech_flag
					clr_country_flag = basic_training_land_tech_flag		
					basic_training_land_tech_revert = 25000
					advanced_training_land_tech = 25000
				}
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						or = {
							and = {
								basic_training_land_tech = 1
								not = { has_country_flag = units_training_law_START }
								not = { training_laws = basic_training }
								training_laws = specialist_training
							}
							and = {
								has_country_flag = basic_training_land_tech_flag
								not = { training_laws = basic_training }
								training_laws = specialist_training
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = units_training_law_START 
					set_country_flag = specialist_training_land_tech_flag
					clr_country_flag = basic_training_land_tech_flag		
					basic_training_land_tech_revert = 25000
					specialist_training_land_tech = 25000
				}
			
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						or = {

								has_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag
								not = { naval_units_training_laws = specialist_training_naval }
								naval_units_training_laws = basic_training_naval
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = naval_units_training_law_START 
					set_country_flag = basic_training_naval_tech_flag
					clr_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag			
					specialist_training_naval_tech_revert = 25000
					naval_basic_training_tech = 25000
				}
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						or = {
							and = {
								specialist_training_naval_tech = 1
								not = { has_country_flag = naval_units_training_law_START }
								not = { naval_units_training_laws = specialist_training_naval }
								naval_units_training_laws = advanced_training_naval
							}
							and = {
								has_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag
								not = { naval_units_training_laws = specialist_training_naval }
								naval_units_training_laws = advanced_training_naval
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = naval_units_training_law_START 
					set_country_flag = advanced_training_naval_tech_flag
					clr_country_flag = specialist_training_naval_tech_flag			
					specialist_training_naval_tech_revert = 25000
					advanced_training_naval_tech = 25000
				}
			}
		}
	}

	id = 24001
		
	is_triggered_only = yes

	desc = ""
	picture = ""

	
	option = {
		name = "OK" # ok
			OMG = {
				any_country = {
					random_owned = {
						limit = {
							air_base = 1
							not = { air_base = 2 }
							not = { fake_air_base = 4 }
						}
						fake_air_base = 4
					}
					random_owned = {
						limit = {
							air_base = 2
							not = { air_base = 3 }
							not = { fake_air_base = 8 }
						}

					}
